### Post by rsavage on 2015-02-26
Beta link - [http://cdimage.ubuntu.com/ubuntu-mate/releases/vivid/beta-1/](http://cdimage.ubuntu.com/ubuntu-mate/releases/vivid/beta-1/)

Notes - [https://ubuntu-mate.org/blog/ubuntu-mate-vivid-beta1/](https://ubuntu-mate.org/blog/ubuntu-mate-vivid-beta1/)

Same rules apply as to 14.10 etc, if you have a radeon card then you need to force pci mode to stop freezing.

Tracker - [http://iso.qa.ubuntu.com/qatracker/milestones/334/builds/89692/testcases](http://iso.qa.ubuntu.com/qatracker/milestones/334/builds/89692/testcases)

### Post by rican-linux on 2015-03-07
Well come to find out that my CD rom on the iBook G4 is not working. So I needed ot boot from CD. However when I tried these two parameters,

```
live-nosplash-powerpc "video=ofonly radeon.agpmode=-1" or live "video=ofonly radeon.modeset=1 radeon.agpmpde=-1" or live "video=offb:off video=radeonfb:off radeon.modeset=1 radeon.agpmode=-1"
```

Ubuntu-MATE will fail to boot. However if I use this,

```
live radeon.modeset=1
```

I can the desktop however if I launch firefox the screen freezes per the reported bug in the known issues page of the wiki. I am posting a screenshot of boot (see attached). I keep getting that '-1' is an invalid paremter for agpmode. Any thoughts?

[ATTACH=CONFIG]260517[/ATTACH]

---

### Post by rican-linux on 2015-03-08
I found my problem I needed to remove the quotes this worked perfectly. I am now installing MATE. :p

```
live radeon.modeset=1 video=offb:off video=radeonfb:off video=1024x768-32 radeon.agpmode=-1
```

---

### Post by rican-linux on 2015-03-09
I got Ubuntu-MATE running on my iBook G4.  I was able to get 3D acceleration working with the r300 driver patch for 14.04 [here]("https://ubuntu-mate.community/t/powerpc-14-04-release-notes/68/2"). However installing them was a download from the 15.04 drivers so when I tried to install software from the software center it upgrade the packages and broke 3D. ### Post by xeno74 on 2015-03-12
Hi All,

I updated my ubuntu MATE 15.04 today. It was a big update. Upstart was removed. And the new Xorg doesn't work.

I installed it again:

Download:

```

wget http://launchpadlibrarian.net/184472691/xserver-xorg-video-radeon_7.4.0-2ubuntu2_powerpc.deb

```

```

wget http://launchpadlibrarian.net/197425102/xserver-xorg-core_1.16.0-1ubuntu1.3_powerpc.deb

```

```

apt-get install upstart

```

```

dpkg -i xserver-xorg-core_1.16.0-1ubuntu1.3_powerpc.deb

```

```

dpkg -i xserver-xorg-video-radeon_7.4.0-2ubuntu2_powerpc.deb

```

Xorg works again.

Rgds,

Christian

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-03-13
There was some problems with the last update of ubuntu MATE 15.04 (see above) yesterday. I had to downgrade Xorg and reinstall upstart. After that I had to copy the unofficial Mesa libs. I created a package with all debs and Mesa libs for the downgrade today.

Download: [Xorg_and_unofficial_Mesa_for_ubuntu_MATE_15.04_AMIGA_one_X1000.tar.gz](http://www.xenosoft.de/Xorg_and_unofficial_Mesa_for_ubuntu_MATE_15.04_AMIGA_one_X1000.tar.gz)

Readme:

> 
After the update of ubuntu Mate 15.04 or Lubuntu 15.04 you have to install some old Xorg packages to get a working X11. The ubuntu MATE 15.04 desktop has some problems with systemd. You have to install upstart to get a full functional ubuntu MATE 15.04 desktop.

1. sudo apt-get install upstart

2. sudo dpkg -i xserver-xorg-core_1.16.0-1ubuntu1.3_powerpc.deb

3. sudo dpkg -i xserver-xorg-video-radeon_7.4.0-2ubuntu2_powerpc.deb

4. Reboot your AMIGA one X1000

If you need 3D acceleration then you have to install the unofficial Mesa.

1. Extract MesaLib-10.0.4-powerpc-unofficial.tar.bz2

2. Rename the original r600_dri.so to r600_dri.so.bak: sudo mv /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/dri/r600_dri.so /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/dri/r600_dri.so.bak

3. Copy the patched r600_dri.so to /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/dri: sudo cp mesa-10.0.4/lib/dri/r600_dri.so /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/dri

4. Rename the original LibGL.so.1.2.0 to LibGL.so.1.2.0.bak: sudo mv /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/mesa/libGL.so.1.2.0 /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/mesa/libGL.so.1.2.0.bak

5. Copy the patched LibGL.so.1.2.0 to /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/mesa: sudo cp mesa-10.0.4/lib/LibGL.so.1.2.0 /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/mesa

6. You can test it with glxgears: vblank_mode=0 glxgears

Tip: You can install the packages above via SSH if you like ;-) 


---

### Post by rican-linux on 2015-03-17
Ok for sound check to see if you have this file /etc/modprobe.d/blacklist.local.conf if so then delete. Next run these commands

```
sudo modprobe snd-aoa-i2sbus
alsamixer
```

If alsamixer comes up make sure your PCM channel is set to 80. I hope this helps!

---

### Post by rican-linux on 2015-03-17
Another thing this i am seeing with 15.04 is video playback is sluggish. mplayer just completely crashes. Well looks like I am going to be doing some more bug reporting! :D

---

### Post by Spectre660 on 2015-03-17
For audio make sure that you add yourself to the group audio .
Also with systemd there can be a delay of about 15 minutes before the audo works.
Observed with Sam460ex and both Debian Jessie and Lubuntu 15.04 and Mate .

### Post by Spectre660 on 2015-03-17
You can try installing ffmpeg and  using fmplay for video playback.
I had to compile versions of mplayer without altivec for my Sam460ex.
Versions work ok in windowed mode on Lubuntu 14.04 and Debian Jessie but could not get one working under Lubuntu 15.04  so I opted for ffplay .

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-03-19
I updated ubuntu MATE 15.04 on my AMIGA one X1000 today. Synaptic told me that it want to remove xserver-xorg-video-radeon and xserver-xorg-video-ati. But there are new versions available (xserver-xorg-video-radeon 1:7.5.0-1ubuntu2 and xserver-xorg-video-ati 1:7.5.0-1ubuntu2). Synaptic removed both old packages and Xorg didn't work after that. I selected both new packages and updated them manually. After a restart I had a black screen with a blink cursor. There aren't any error messages in the log file **/var/log/Xorg.0.log** but I found some error messages in the log file **/var/log/syslog**:

```

. Exiting.
Mar 19 11:45:41 ubuntu systemd[1]: lightdm.service: main process exited, code=exited, status=1/FAILURE
Mar 19 11:45:41 ubuntu systemd[1]: Unit lightdm.service entered failed state.
Mar 19 11:45:41 ubuntu systemd[1]: lightdm.service failed.
Mar 19 11:45:41 ubuntu systemd[1]: lightdm.service holdoff time over, scheduling restart.
Mar 19 11:45:41 ubuntu systemd[1]: Starting Light Display Manager...
Mar 19 11:45:41 ubuntu systemd[1]: Started Light Display Manager.
Mar 19 11:45:41 ubuntu lightdm[20218]: initctl: Verbindung zu Upstart nicht möglich: Failed to connect to socket /com/ubuntu/upstart: Verbindungsaufbau abgelehnt
Mar 19 11:45:42 ubuntu systemd[1]: Started Session c109 of user lightdm.
Mar 19 11:45:42 ubuntu systemd[1]: Starting Session c109 of user lightdm.
Mar 19 11:45:42 ubuntu lightdm[20218]: ** (lightdm:20218): WARNING **: Error using VT_WAITACTIVE 7 on /dev/console: No such device or address
Mar 19 11:45:43 ubuntu kernel: lightdm-gtk-gre[20251]: unhandled signal 11 at 00000000 nip 6f4e61c4 lr 6f4e619c code 30001
Mar 19 11:45:44 ubuntu org.gtk.vfs.Daemon[20250]: A connection to the bus can't be made
Mar 19 11:45:44 ubuntu org.gtk.vfs.Daemon[20250]: g_dbus_connection_real_closed: Remote peer vanished with error: Underlying GIOStream returned 0 bytes on an async read (g-io-error-quark, 0). Exiting.
Mar 19 11:45:44 ubuntu systemd[1]: lightdm.service: main process exited, code=exited, status=1/FAILURE
Mar 19 11:45:44 ubuntu systemd[1]: Unit lightdm.service entered failed state.
Mar 19 11:45:44 ubuntu systemd[1]: lightdm.service failed.
Mar 19 11:45:44 ubuntu systemd[1]: lightdm.service holdoff time over, scheduling restart.
Mar 19 11:45:44 ubuntu systemd[1]: Starting Light Display Manager...
Mar 19 11:45:44 ubuntu systemd[1]: Started Light Display Manager.
Mar 19 11:45:44 ubuntu lightdm[20381]: initctl: Verbindung zu Upstart nicht möglich: Failed to connect to socket /com/ubuntu/upstart: Verbindungsaufbau abgelehnt
Mar 19 11:45:45 ubuntu systemd[1]: Started Session c110 of user lightdm.
Mar 19 11:45:45 ubuntu systemd[1]: Starting Session c110 of user lightdm.
Mar 19 11:45:45 ubuntu lightdm[20381]: ** (lightdm:20381): WARNING **: Error using VT_WAITACTIVE 7 on /dev/console: No such device or address
Mar 19 11:45:46 ubuntu kernel: lightdm-gtk-gre[20414]: unhandled signal 11 at 00000000 nip 6f4e61c4 lr 6f4e619c code 30001
Mar 19 11:45:46 ubuntu org.gtk.vfs.Daemon[20413]: A connection to the bus can't be made
Mar 19 11:45:46 ubuntu org.gtk.vfs.Daemon[20413]: g_dbus_connection_real_closed: Remote peer vanished with error: Underlying GIOStream returned 0 bytes on an async read (g-io-error-quark, 0)

```

The temporary solution is to downgrade Xorg:

```

sudo dpkg -i xserver-xorg-core_1.16.0-1ubuntu1.3_powerpc.deb

```

```

sudo dpkg -i xserver-xorg-video-radeon_7.4.0-2ubuntu2_powerpc.deb

```

```

sudo dpkg -i xserver-xorg-video-ati_7.4.0-2ubuntu2_powerpc.deb

```

I created a package with all debs and Mesa libs for the downgrade last week.

Download: [Xorg_and_unofficial_Mesa_for_ubuntu_MATE_15.04_AMIGA_one_X1000.tar.gz]("http://www.xenosoft.de/Xorg_and_unofficial_Mesa_for_ubuntu_MATE_15.04_AMIGA_one_X1000.tar.gz")

I created a bug report on bugs.launchpad today. Link: [Bug #1434036 ubuntu MATE 15.04 PPC/Lubuntu 15.04 PPC Xorg: Only black screen with blink cursor after update]("https://bugs.launchpad.net/ubuntu/+source/xserver-xorg-video-ati/+bug/1434036").

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-03-20
I tried **systemd** again today.

```
sudo apt-get install systemd-sysv
``` 

If you install the package **systemd-sysv** then **Upstart** will _removed_ and **systemd** will installed as a _default init system_.

With **systemd** you don't need the **rw** boot argument but unfortunately the **mate-settings-daemon** doesn't work (see screenshot).

[[IMG]http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/download/file.php?id=1620&t=1[/IMG]](http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/download/file.php?id=1620&mode=view)

I had to reinstall Upstart.

```
sudo apt-get install upstart
```

After that, the **mate-settings-daemon** works without any problems.

---

### Post by rican-linux on 2015-03-20
I knew this looked familar! I was running into similar issues when I testing Debian Jessie (I had a thread on the Debian forums [here]("http://forums.debian.net/viewtopic.php?f=10&t=119267").) So for atk and gail make sure you have these packages installed (assuming ubuntu has the same packages and I know you probably do not need the dgb packages). This should fix those modules failing to load, hopfully that should fix the other issue. Let me know!

```
rican-linux@debian-ppc:~$ dpkg -l |grep gail
ii libgail-3-0:powerpc 3.14.4-2 powerpc GNOME Accessibility Implementation Library -- shared libraries
ii libgail-3-0-dbg:powerpc 3.14.4-2 powerpc Gail libraries and debugging symbols
ii libgail-3-dev:powerpc 3.14.4-2 powerpc GNOME Accessibility Implementation Library -- development files
ii libgail-3-doc 3.14.4-2 all documentation files of the Gail library
ii libgail-common:powerpc 2.24.25-1 powerpc GNOME Accessibility Implementation Library -- common modules
ii libgail-dbg:powerpc 2.24.25-1 powerpc Gail libraries and debugging symbols
ii libgail-dev 2.24.25-1 powerpc GNOME Accessibility Implementation Library -- development files
ii libgail-doc 2.24.25-1 all documentation files of the Gail library
ii libgail18:powerpc 2.24.25-1 powerpc GNOME Accessibility Implementation Library -- shared libraries
rican-linux@debian-ppc:~$ dpkg -l |grep atk
ii gir1.2-atk-1.0 2.14.0-1 powerpc ATK accessibility toolkit (GObject introspection)
ii libatk-adaptor:powerpc 2.14.0-2 powerpc AT-SPI 2 toolkit bridge
ii libatk-adaptor-data 2.14.0-2 all AT-SPI 2 toolkit bridge - transitional dummy package
ii libatk-adaptor-dbg:powerpc 2.14.0-2 powerpc AT-SPI 2 toolkit bridge - debugging symbols
ii libatk-bridge2.0-0:powerpc 2.14.0-2 powerpc AT-SPI 2 toolkit bridge - shared library
ii libatk-bridge2.0-0-dbg:powerpc 2.14.0-2 powerpc AT-SPI 2 toolkit bridge - debugging symbols
ii libatk-bridge2.0-dev:powerpc 2.14.0-2 powerpc Development files for the AT-SPI 2 toolkit bridge
ii libatk-wrapper-java 0.30.5-1 all ATK implementation for Java using JNI
ii libatk-wrapper-java-jni:powerpc 0.30.5-1 powerpc ATK implementation for Java using JNI (JNI bindings)
ii libatk1.0-0:powerpc 2.14.0-1 powerpc ATK accessibility toolkit
ii libatk1.0-data 2.14.0-1 all Common files for the ATK accessibility toolkit
ii libatk1.0-dbg:powerpc 2.14.0-1 powerpc ATK libraries and debugging symbols
ii libatk1.0-dev 2.14.0-1 powerpc Development files for the ATK accessibility toolkit
ii libatk1.0-doc 2.14.0-1 all Documentation files for the ATK toolkit
ii libatk3.0-cil 2.99.3-2 powerpc CLI binding for the ATK accessibility toolkit
ii libatkmm-1.6-1:powerpc 2.22.7-2.1 powerpc C++ wrappers for ATK accessibility toolkit (shared libraries)
ii libatkmm-1.6-dbg:powerpc 2.22.7-2.1 powerpc C++ wrappers for ATK accessibility toolkit (debug symbols)
ii libatkmm-1.6-dev:powerpc 2.22.7-2.1 powerpc C++ wrappers for ATK accessibility toolkit (development files)
ii libatkmm-1.6-doc 2.22.7-2.1 all C++ wrappers for ATK accessibility toolkit (documentation)
```

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-03-27
> **xeno74 said:**
> 
Just for info: Since  the last update I can't activate Upstart. I have to use systemd. With  systemd, the mate-settings-daemon starts 10 minutes later after the  desktop login. It means it works but I have to wait 10 minutes after the  login.


I found a way to reactivate Upstart. :-) You can reactivate Upstart with **sudo apt-get install upstart-sysv**. After that the **mate-settings-daemon** works without any problems.

> **luigiburdo said:**

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-03-29
> **luigiburdo said:**
> Xeno74,
nothing to do ... 
loading from cd i have the mate splash on RadeonHD 
after 
black screen blinking when the system load.


The temporary solution is to downgrade Xorg:

```

sudo dpkg -i xserver-xorg-core_1.16.0-1ubuntu1.3_powerpc.deb

```

```

sudo dpkg -i xserver-xorg-video-radeon_7.4.0-2ubuntu2_powerpc.deb

```

```

sudo dpkg -i xserver-xorg-video-ati_7.4.0-2ubuntu2_powerpc.deb

```

I created a package with all debs and Mesa libs for the downgrade three weeks ago.

Download: [Xorg_and_unofficial_Mesa_for_ubuntu_MATE_15.04_AMIGA_one_X1000.tar.gz]("http://www.xenosoft.de/Xorg_and_unofficial_Mesa_for_ubuntu_MATE_15.04_AMIGA_one_X1000.tar.gz")

I created a bug report on bugs.launchpad two weeks ago. Link: [Bug #1434036 ubuntu MATE 15.04 PPC/Lubuntu 15.04 PPC Xorg: Only black screen with blink cursor after update]("https://bugs.launchpad.net/ubuntu/+source/xserver-xorg-video-ati/+bug/1434036").

> **luigiburdo said:**
> 
i try to switch on tty and there was asking an username and password (???)

i cant test it whitout username and password...

Username is **ubuntu-mate**. No password.

Please try it out.

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-03-30
I asked Adam Smith the follwing question:

> 
Do you want to release ubuntu MATE 15.04 PowerPC as an official release in April?&#65279;


Adam Smith told me yesterday:

>  
The plan from the ubuntu mate team is to release a PowerPC iso, but that will only happen if it is tested and passes.  Currently the beta2 is unusable and so I wouldn't release the final version if it has the same problems.  This won't stop you installing via the mini iso and playing with various versions of the xorg. Personally I have no time to devote to this (and rarely use my PowerPC machine), so if PowerPC people want an iso then they need to test and bug hunt/bash.&#65279;


Quote Martin Wimpress:

>  
Can you powerpc guys head over to [http://iso.qa.ubuntu.com](http://iso.qa.ubuntu.com) and please. I can't get it going on my G4 :(


Quote Adam Smith:

> 
Yep, powerpc seems to be broken....the xorg seems to be be continually restarting and some colours are wrong.  Was that the problem you ran into?&#65279;


Quote Martin Wimpress:

> 
Yes, that is what I experienced :(


Source: [ubuntu MATE google+]("https://plus.google.com/u/0/communities/108331279007926658904")

I tested the [beta 2 PowerPC]("http://cdimage.ubuntu.com/ubuntu-mate/releases/15.04/beta-2/ubuntu-mate-15.04-beta2-desktop-powerpc.iso") in a virtual QEMU/KVM machine. Please kindly request that the users affects by this issue Confirm the LP bug and add the comments to the LP bug. The information about modesetting is particularly relevant in the case, since was radically changed in Xorg 1.17.

It is no use discussing this in the forums, the Canonical developers do not look there &#128546; Please get all the relevant information into LP and encourage the rest of the PowerPC community to do the same &#9786;&#65279;


LP bug report 1: [Bug #1434036 ubuntu MATE 15.04 PPC/Lubuntu 15.04 PPC Xorg: Only black screen with blink cursor after update]("https://bugs.launchpad.net/ubuntu/+source/xserver-xorg-video-ati/+bug/1434036")

### Post by este.el.paz on 2015-03-30
> [COLOR=#888888][COLOR=#000000]I then tried a Feb  6??? iso of Vivid PPC that I believe booted with the "agp" params OK in  my iBook . . . and we slowly (450 MHz processor) got to a desktop with  the Lu background symbol . . . but kind of rough res images, and just  the trash can and "install" icons on the desktop . . . icon ID words  were not read-able and the "LXDE" launcher applet never appeared.  While  I was trying to figure out how to set the system time it seemed like  the system and my screen "went to sleep" . . . screen went black and the  power button turned orange from its active blue.  Could not revive the  situation . . . shut down with the power button.[/COLOR][/COLOR]

Posted this informal report to the Lu user list about testing 15.04 on a G4 Sawtooth.  For PPC users it's one of those chicken v egg things . . . so many issues just with getting it to run that it renders continued testing somewhat questionable . . . then devs and such can say, "See, the PPC people aren't testing" . . . and then the lack of enthusiasm just creates a death spiral . . . .  There are people testing PPC, enough to get some serious attention for continuing development . . . but it seems like even the i386 folks are finding issues with 15.04 . . . lots of work needed, etc.

e...

[edit:  Just checked the Lu users qa list to make sure that I remembered seeing that Lu is only working on LTS versions for PPC, and so that means that Vivid is not going to get a whole lot of PPC attention . . . if any.  Possibly bug reports that are effecting universally will be dealt with . . . .]

[[IMG]http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/download/file.php?id=1662&t=1[/IMG]]("http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/download/file.php?id=1662&mode=view")

The temporary solution for QEMU and Power Macs is, to try to install ubuntu MATE 15.04 with the Ubuntu Server ISO. The installer runs only in text mode.

Download: [vivid-server-powerpc.iso]("http://cdimage.ubuntu.com/ubuntu-server/daily/current/vivid-server-powerpc.iso")

If you installed it, then you could install the ubuntu MATE packages and the OpenSSH server. After that you could downgrade Xorg via SSH. What do you think?

[quote="xeno74"]
I created a package with all debs and Mesa libs for the downgrade last week.

Download: [Xorg_and_unofficial_Mesa_for_ubuntu_MATE_15.04_AMIGA_one_X1000.tar.gz](http://www.xenosoft.de/Xorg_and_unofficial_Mesa_for_ubuntu_MATE_15.04_AMIGA_one_X1000.tar.gz)

I created a bug report on bugs.launchpad today. Link: [Bug #1434036 ubuntu MATE 15.04 PPC/Lubuntu 15.04 PPC Xorg: Only black screen with blink cursor after update](https://bugs.launchpad.net/ubuntu/+source/xserver-xorg-video-ati/+bug/1434036).[/quote]

[quote="Adam Smith (adamsmith)"]
There are a lot of unhandled signal 11 errors in those logs - could you confirm if you all have those so we're talking about the same error? If downgrading the xorg packages fixes those errors[/quote]

Yes, the downgrade fixes the signal 11 errors. I figured out that I have a lot of signal 11 error messages with systemd. With Upstart I have only 4 signal 11 errors:

```

[ 9.371697] lightdm-gtk-gre[2731]: unhandled signal 11 at 00000000 nip 6f4e61c4 lr 6f4e619c code 30001
[ 14.367464] lightdm-gtk-gre[3000]: unhandled signal 11 at 00000000 nip 6f4e61c4 lr 6f4e619c code 30001
[ 20.591891] lightdm-gtk-gre[3219]: unhandled signal 11 at 00000000 nip 6f4e61c4 lr 6f4e619c code 30001
[ 26.831432] lightdm-gtk-gre[3533]: unhandled signal 11 at 00000000 nip 6f4e61c4 lr 6f4e619c code 30001

```

With systemd, X11 starts again and again with a white screen. With Upstart I have a black screen with a blink cursor.

I added some log files to the LP bug report today.

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-04-08
> **luigiburdo said:**
> 
look like now on AmigaOne X1000 it is strarting  not working too before was the most linux compatible ppc machine.

Luigi,

Unfortunately you're right. This Xorg bug effects all PowerPC machines. The AMIGA one X1000 users use the old Xorg packages. [[1]]("http://www.xenosoft.de/Xorg_and_unofficial_Mesa_for_ubuntu_MATE_15.04_AMIGA_one_X1000.tar.gz") I updated both bug reports with this information today. [[2]]("https://bugs.launchpad.net/ubuntu/+source/xserver-xorg-video-ati/+bug/1434036") [[3]]("https://bugs.freedesktop.org/show_bug.cgi?id=89862").

@All

zzd10h tested the new **RC7** of kernel 4.0 with the old Xorg packages and with MATE 15.04 PowerPC successfully on his AMIGA one X1000 yesterday.

[[IMG]http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/download/file.php?id=1675&t=1[/IMG]]("http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/download/file.php?id=1675&mode=view")

Cheers,

Christian

### Post by luigiburdo on 2015-04-16
Dont worry about the rtc0 errors it because the kernel try to find rtc of power5 up clock and isnt present on powermacs.

dont use live video=ofonly ... use : 

```

live video=offb:off video=nouveaufb:off nouveau.modeset=1


```

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-04-20
I updated **ubuntu MATE 15.04** PowerPC on my A-EON AMIGA one X1000 today. In 3 days is the official release day for ubuntu MATE 15.04. My installed Upstart was not replaced by the Software Updater. Xorg works but the icons in the MATE panel and in the MATE menus have wrong colors. The icons on the desktop have right colors. I downgraded Xorg to version 1.16.0.

```

dpkg -i xserver-xorg-core_1.16.0-1ubuntu1.3_powerpc.deb
dpkg -i xserver-xorg-video-radeon_7.4.0-2ubuntu2_powerpc.deb

```

After a new login (not restart) all icons have the right colors.

You can find these debs in the following package:

[img]http://www.supertuxkart-amiga.de/amiga/Mesa-X1000.jpg[/img]

[Xorg_and_unofficial_Mesa_for_ubuntu_MATE_15.04_AMIGA_one_X1000.tar.gz](http://www.xenosoft.de/Xorg_and_unofficial_Mesa_for_ubuntu_MATE_15.04_AMIGA_one_X1000.tar.gz)

Interesting, after the update it doesn't called 'development version'. It's _Ubuntu 15.04_. :-) I tested the unofficial Mesa 10.0.4 with 'glxgears' and with SuperTuxKart 0.8.1 AltiVec. It works without any problems. You can find the unofficial Mesa 10.0.4 in the package above too. Audio/sound works very well too.

Conclusion

ubuntu MATE works perfect with Upstart, Xorg 1.16.0, and the unofficial Mesa 10.0.4 currently. I hope the developers fix the problems with Xorg, systemd, and Mesa in the future. I can recommend you the package [Xorg_and_unofficial_Mesa_for_ubuntu_MATE_15.04_AMIGA_one_X1000.tar.gz](http://www.xenosoft.de/Xorg_and_unofficial_Mesa_for_ubuntu_MATE_15.04_AMIGA_one_X1000.tar.gz). It includes all packages for a very well working ubuntu MATE 15.04 PowerPC. ;-) I want to test ubuntu MATE 15.04 further after the release.

[[IMG]http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/download/file.php?id=1698&t=1[/IMG]]("http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/download/file.php?id=1698&mode=view")

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-04-25
Hi All,

I read that Mesa 10.5 is faster with a Radeon HD6870 than the older Mesa versions.

Link: [Ubuntu 15.04 Offers Faster OpenGL For AMD Radeon GPUs On Open-Source](http://www.phoronix.com/scan.php?page=article&item=ubuntu-1504-radfast&num=1)

Therefore I patched it because of the wrong colors problem and compiled it on my AMIGA one X1000 today. I tested the new Mesa 10.5.4 with 'glxgears' and with SuperTuxKart 0.8.1 on Debian Sid. Unfortunately STK is slower with the new Mesa. At least 15% slower than with the unofficial Mesa 10.0.4. 3D acceleration works but slower on Debian Sid.

The unofficial Mesa 10.0.4 is used on some Power Macs and on the AMIGA one X1000 because all new official Mesa versions on Linux PPC have wrong colors.

More information about Mesa on Linux PPC: [forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz](http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/viewtopic.php?f=35&t=2137)

Rgds,

Christian

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-05-20
> **este.el.paz said:**
> @xeno:

Appreciate the details . . . I found out from "smiffy" on the U-MATE forum that there are "big endian problems with Xorg 1.7," with a suggestion that some users in Powerpc have gone back to Xorg 1.6 on the G+ community or group . . . .  Haven't had time to check into that yet . . . .

e..

Yes, I created a Xorg 1.16 package with all debs and Mesa libs for the downgrade two months ago.

Download: [Xorg_and_unofficial_Mesa_for_ubuntu_MATE_15.04_AMIGA_one_X1000.tar.gz](http://www.xenosoft.de/Xorg_and_unofficial_Mesa_for_ubuntu_MATE_15.04_AMIGA_one_X1000.tar.gz)

Readme:

> 
After the update of ubuntu Mate 15.04 or Lubuntu 15.04 you have to install some old Xorg packages to get a working X11. The ubuntu MATE 15.04 desktop has some problems with systemd. You have to install upstart to get a full functional ubuntu MATE 15.04 desktop.

1. sudo apt-get install upstart-sysv

2. sudo dpkg -i xserver-xorg-core_1.16.0-1ubuntu1.3_powerpc.deb

3. sudo dpkg -i xserver-xorg-video-radeon_7.4.0-2ubuntu2_powerpc.deb

4. Reboot your PowerPC computer

If you need 3D acceleration then you have to install the unofficial Mesa.

1. Extract MesaLib-10.0.4-powerpc-unofficial.tar.bz2

2. Rename the original r600_dri.so to r600_dri.so.bak: sudo mv /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/dri/r600_dri.so /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/dri/r600_dri.so.bak

3. Copy the patched r600_dri.so to /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/dri: sudo cp mesa-10.0.4/lib/dri/r600_dri.so /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/dri

4. Rename the original LibGL.so.1.2.0 to LibGL.so.1.2.0.bak: sudo mv /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/mesa/libGL.so.1.2.0 /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/mesa/libGL.so.1.2.0.bak

5. Copy the patched LibGL.so.1.2.0 to /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/mesa: sudo cp mesa-10.0.4/lib/LibGL.so.1.2.0 /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/mesa

6. You can test it with glxgears: vblank_mode=0 glxgears

Tip: You can install the packages above via SSH if you like ;-) 


I tested Compiz with ubuntu MATE 15.04 PowerPC today. Compiz is an OpenGL composite and window manager. You can activate it with MATE Tweak. Compiz works very well with the unofficial Mesa.

[[IMG]http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/download/file.php?id=1737&t=1[/IMG]]("http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/download/file.php?id=1737&mode=view")

### Post by rican-linux on 2015-07-15
The off colors are due to a bug in xorg 1.17.1-2 the fix is version 1.17.2-1 but that is only available in Sid. If you want a stable system you could try 14.04 lubuntu. 

Did you try to add these setting when you loaded Jessie?

```
Linux radeon.modeset=1 video=offb:off video=radeonfb:off radeon.agpmode=-1
```

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-07-26
Hi All,

After a big update today I found two problems in ubuntu MATE 15.10 PowerPC today.

The first is systemd. If I start ubuntu MATE 15.10 with systemd then the gnome-settings daemon doesn't start and MATE Tweak doesn't work (see screenshot). If I use upstart-sysv then MATE Tweak and the gnome-settings-daeomon work without any problems.

[https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/-thH5wqTr4ck/VbTKSDJrDuI/AAAAAAAAA3M/SB0MYp1oSwU/w1245-h934-no/systemd-sysv_problem_ubuntu_MATE_15.10_PowerPC.png](https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/-thH5wqTr4ck/VbTKSDJrDuI/AAAAAAAAA3M/SB0MYp1oSwU/w1245-h934-no/systemd-sysv_problem_ubuntu_MATE_15.10_PowerPC.png)

Additionally there is a problem with MATE Tweak itself. If I switch to Compiz then it set org.gnome.metacity theme to 'Ambiant-MATE'. Metacity can't display the window decoration with the two apostrophes in the theme name (see screenshot). 

[https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-Yx71_2ogB-Q/VbTKZhUU4sI/AAAAAAAAA3Y/j9vlqLpVWJ4/w1245-h934-no/metacity_problem_ubuntu_MATE_15.10_PowerPC.png](https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-Yx71_2ogB-Q/VbTKZhUU4sI/AAAAAAAAA3Y/j9vlqLpVWJ4/w1245-h934-no/metacity_problem_ubuntu_MATE_15.10_PowerPC.png)

I created an own script to switch to Compiz and I set the theme name without apostrophes:

```

gsettings set org.gnome.metacity theme Ambiant-MATE
compiz --replace

```

This works very well.

Further information: [https://plus.google.com/115515624056477014971/posts/5NRovNknxRw]("https://plus.google.com/115515624056477014971/posts/5NRovNknxRw")


Rgds,

Christian&#65279;

---

### Post by este.el.paz on 2015-07-27
Folks:

Tested U-MATE 15.10 Alpha for PPC spun on 6/25/15 (Merican dating) . . . also found "issues" on my iBook G4 933MHz.  The MATE blurb said "kms is enabled" but booting "live" seemed at first to be "OK" . . . but, launching Terminal to run apt update the bottom part of the window was blurred out, couldn't see if it was still loading sources, then the screen flashed to black and back to showing display, screen "froze" cursor was stuck in clench mode and couldn't break out of it or drag window . . . that went on until I shut it down.

Rebooting but this time using boot params that I've used "live video=ofonly radeon agpmode=-1" . . . and things were "better" . . . no screen freeze, Terminal window was fully operational, but display colors were "off" and the white cursor would "disappear" . . . Facebook pages were not loading, a few other issues . . . (notes at home) . . . and then shutting down out of live session didn't "reboot" . . . it just "hung" . . . had to shut down with power button.  

So, some things very good, fonts were well rendered, but . . . not exactly ready for primetime in this version for PPC . . . and it didn't seem like kms was enabled out of the box.  Also, got the "i2c" error . . . no sound . . . .

e..

It's just got 646 MB RAM, doesn't seem to be enough to do anything on the net . . . 933 MHz is blowing its top.  Even basic LXDE seems to be taking all its got and giving me noise.  But, back to the testing of 15.10 alpha . . . didn't seem to get it working in the color rendering area too well.  Otherwise, OK, no flashing black display or frozen screen as with the "live" boot param.

e..

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-08-05
Musa told me the following news about his Power Mac G5:

> 
Hi Christian. I just want to tell you that it has succeeded for me to get full 3D support on my powermac g5 radeon 9550. Since it is not amiga related I write it as a private message to you. At the beginning of my mate 15.10 installation I could not get the radeon driver to load. Then I read somewhere that I could rename /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/dri/r300_dri.so so that the system could not find it. It meant that I had suddenly have software GL. but so Slooooov :) Then I got the idea to take r300_dri.so from your mesa software package AmigaX1000 and replace the old ... BINGO now I have 3D support for my Radeon 9550. The system is not as fast as my X1000 but certainly usable. Regards Peter (Musa)

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-08-13
**Installing the unofficial Mesa on ubuntu MATE 15.10, Lubuntu 15.10, and Xubuntu 15.10**

Download: [MesaLib-10.0.4-powerpc-unofficial.tar.bz2]("http://www.xenosoft.de/MesaLib-10.0.4-powerpc-unofficial.tar.bz2")

[LIST=1]
[*]sudo mv /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/dri/r600_dri.so /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/dri/r600_dri.so.bak
[*]sudo cp mesa-10.0.4/lib/dri/r600_dri.so /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/dri
[*]sudo mv /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/mesa/libGL.so.1.2.0 /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/mesa/libGL.so.1.2.0.bak
[*]sudo cp mesa-10.0.4/lib/libGL.so.1.2.0 /usr/lib/powerpc-linux-gnu/mesa
[/LIST]

---

[QUOTE=corto]
I also tested Ubuntu Mate 15.10 Alpha 2, on a MacMini at the moment. Here are my first comments:
- I also had a crash of the Welcome app. Note: The problem disappeared after I updated the system packages.
- During installation, I had a window saying "The panel encourtered a problem while loading TrashAppletFactory::TrashApplet".
- I don't know if colors are right during the boot, this is rather blue. I confirm that on a shutdown, colors are wrong.
-  The main problem: After a while, the system slowdowns, freezes and then  starts a slow flickering. And I've just tested: it happens immediately  when I run glxgears. If I use "radeon.agmode=-1" on the boot command  line, glgears works at 58 FPS (but when the desktop appears, I have a  resilient terminal background displayed at the top left of the screen).  With both "radeon.agmode=-1" and "video=offb:off", glxgears runs at 61  FPS and the display looks good.
- KMS is enabled and GL renderer is MESA DRI R200. MESA version is 10.5.9.
-  After some inactivity, the screen blanker runs and if I move the mouse,  I am invited to enter my password. When done and clicked on "Unlock",  it displays the screen blanker again ! And if I move the mouse, etc.  There is a [bug report here]("https://bugs.launchpad.net/ubuntu-mate/+bug/1471454") that says it is fixed in Mate 1.10 but this version is reached after a full packages update and that still fails.
[/QUOTE]

Link: [amigaworld.net]("http://amigaworld.net/modules/newbb/viewtopic.php?topic_id=40435&forum=34&17#766418")

### Post by ernsteiswuerfel on 2015-08-23
Hinted by xeno on a1k.org I tried to install Ubuntu MATE 15.10 PPC on my Powerbook 5,4 and ran into following problems. ;)

1.) On the current alpha-2 ISO yaboot is not installed as package. Which is annoying if you want to use the ISO as a rescue CD to edit and write-back /etc/yaboot.conf manually.

2.) Wanted to use btrfs as root-filesystem but I failed so far. I used a small ext2 partition for /boot/. This part works - vmlinux gets loaded and the kernel starts. For pointing the kernel to the btrfs root-partition on /dev/sda7 I use:```
image=/boot/vmlinux
    label=Linux
    read-only
    initrd=/initrd.img
    root=/dev/sda7/@
    append="radeon.agpmode=-1"
```
in /etc/yaboot.conf which does not work. The "@"-subvolume is automatically created when using btrfs as filesystem for /. When booting I get dropped into busybox after a while because the kernel is not able to find the root partotion. But mounting the btrfs / out of busybox works... :-s

---

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-08-24
> **ernsteiswuerfel said:**
> 
2.) Wanted to use btrfs as root-filesystem but I failed so far. I used a small ext2 partition for /boot/. This part works - vmlinux gets loaded and the kernel starts. For pointing the kernel to the btrfs root-partition on /dev/sda7 I use:```
image=/boot/vmlinux
    label=Linux
    read-only
    initrd=/initrd.img
    root=/dev/sda7/@
    append="radeon.agpmode=-1"
```
in /etc/yaboot.conf which does not work. The "@"-subvolume is automatically created when using btrfs as filesystem for /. When booting I get dropped into busybox after a while because the kernel is not able to find the root partotion. But mounting the btrfs / out of busybox works... :-s

Unfortunately there are some problems with the BTRFS file system. Please look in the following thread: [http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/viewtopic.php?f=35&t=2983&start=30#p34140](http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/viewtopic.php?f=35&t=2983&start=30#p34140)
I can recommend you to use the ext4 file system.

### Post by ernsteiswuerfel on 2015-08-24
> **xeno74 said:**
> Unfortunately there are some problems with the BTRFS file system. Please look in the following thread: [http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/viewtopic.php?f=35&t=2983&start=30#p34140](http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/viewtopic.php?f=35&t=2983&start=30#p34140)
I can recommend you to use the ext4 file system.

I did some more research and finally found the correct parameter to boot into a btrfs /. :D
```
image=/vmlinux
    label=Linux
    read-only
    root=/dev/sda7
    initrd=/initrd.img
    append="**rootflags=subvol=@** radeon.agpmode=-1"


``` 
Running btrfs without issues so far, I even turned lzo filesystem compression on. AFAIK many issues with btrfs have been resolved with kernel > 4.0 and btrfs-progs > 4.0 ([https://btrfs.wiki.kernel.org/index.php/Main_Page#News](https://btrfs.wiki.kernel.org/index.php/Main_Page#News)).

It would be convenient if the yaboot installer-script from the ISO checks if btrfs is used as root-filesystem and adds ```
append="rootflags=subvol=@"
``` to /etc/yaboot.conf automatically.

---

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-08-30

image=/vmlinux
    label=Linux
    read-only
    root=/dev/sda7
    initrd=/initrd.img
    append="**rootflags=subvol=@** radeon.agpmode=-1"


``` 
Running btrfs without issues so far, I even turned lzo filesystem compression on. AFAIK many issues with btrfs have been resolved with kernel > 4.0 and btrfs-progs > 4.0 ([https://btrfs.wiki.kernel.org/index.php/Main_Page#News](https://btrfs.wiki.kernel.org/index.php/Main_Page#News)).

It would be convenient if the yaboot installer-script from the ISO checks if btrfs is used as root-filesystem and adds ```
append="rootflags=subvol=@"
``` to /etc/yaboot.conf automatically.

Hi Luigi,

You could try to use an old Linux kernel from Ubuntu 14.04. You can install the kernel package with "dpkg -i".

Download: [kernel-image-3.13.0-24-powerpc64-smp-di_3.13.0-24.46_powerpc.udeb]("http://launchpadlibrarian.net/172527322/kernel-image-3.13.0-24-powerpc64-smp-di_3.13.0-24.46_powerpc.udeb")

Furthermore you could compile a kernel if you like. ;-)

You could try Upstart instead of systemd with the old kernel if you like.

Installation:

sudo apt-get install upstart-sysv

### Post by Spectre660 on 2015-09-08
Try using the VGA output if you have it on the video card.
 I had a problem with HDMI and DVI output on the Sam460ex starting with kernel 4.03 until a fix in 4.2 got back ported into the 4.1 branch.

[https://git.kernel.org/cgit/linux/kernel/git/torvalds/linux.git/commit/?id=d0ea397e22f9ad0113c1dbdaab14eded050472eb](https://git.kernel.org/cgit/linux/kernel/git/torvalds/linux.git/commit/?id=d0ea397e22f9ad0113c1dbdaab14eded050472eb)

@opepe:

Try to go back to LTS Lu or Xu 14.04, go with whatever works on your machine.  Read the PowerPCFAQ and see if there are any notes for your machine with whatever version you are trying.  I have no problem recommending Xu 12.04 LTS, it more or less just works straight outta the box on PPC, might need an xorg.conf file depending on which machine yours is.  I'm running ToriOS/jwm on top of a xu 12.04 install on a Powermac 3,1??? Sawtooth 450 MHz processor, takes a minute to load and connect to net on FF, but once it does it's very zippy.  I think I saw that 12.04 will get updates until 2017, and ToriOS development is "on the move" right now.  The numix themes are great . . . I don't have acceleration, but, don't need it.

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-10-01
Hi All,

I have very exciting news!!!!!! I could install ubuntu MATE 15.10 PowerPC in a chroot on Lubuntu 12.04.5 PowerPC. I can use the ubuntu MATE 15.10 desktop in fullscreen or I can use the new programs from ubuntu MATE 15.10 on the Lubuntu 12.04.5 desktop. Sound and 3D acceleration works very well in the chroot. This is really fantastic.

If you want to test ubuntu MATE 15.10 with a lot of new programs such as Firefox 41 or LibreOffice 5 and you don't have a free partition or you couldn't install it on your PowerPC computer, then you can install it in a chroot on your existing 12.04 system.

Further information and installation instructions: [http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/viewtopic.php?f=35&t=3055&start=80#p35457](http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/viewtopic.php?f=35&t=3055&start=80#p35457)

[[IMG]https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-CtVV6Jqwudo/Vg0cI29SmQI/AAAAAAAABZk/1scx6IdvGzM/w426-h320/ubuntu_MATE_15.10_PowerPC_chroot_fullscreen.png[/IMG]]("http://forum.hyperion-entertainment.biz/viewtopic.php?f=35&t=3055&start=80#p35457")

[[IMG]https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-FZjAHi3y69s/Vgz8CSQ-zkI/AAAAAAAABYM/mkK1rYFGDOg/s213-p/ubuntu_MATE_15.10_PowerPC_chroot_2.png[/IMG]]("https://plus.google.com/115515624056477014971/posts/5zonoqFDzGW")
[[IMG]https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-qIRWbJ6arUU/Vgz77qjzl3I/AAAAAAAABYE/tJqBsWESrHM/w212-h213-p/ubuntu_MATE_15.10_PowerPC_chroot_1.png[/IMG]]("https://plus.google.com/115515624056477014971/posts/5zonoqFDzGW")

### Post by xeno74 on 2015-10-02
FYI:

**Nouveau modeset no longer works with kernel 4.0 on Power Mac G4**

[QUOTE=Peter Saisanas]
Hi,

I have posted a message on the debian powerpc mailing list recently regarding the nouveau issues along with creating a bug report for the nouveau developers to look into. Within the freedesktop nouveau bug report, a nouveau dev explains why it is failing to work in more recent kernels.


Post below, link within for nouveau bug report.
[https://lists.debian.org/debian-powerpc/2015/07/msg00026.html](https://lists.debian.org/debian-powerpc/2015/07/msg00026.html)

As a workaround, i have been able to get it up and running by using an equivalent x86 vga bios for the exact card that you have (in my case i have a Quadro FX4500). Not ideal, but gets you running till the bug gets fixed.


Simply download the equivalent x86 vga bios for your particular card, save file within /lib/firmware.

In my case i saved the x86 vga bios as quadro_fx4500.fw .

pass the following option to the nouveau module (change the to the filename as saved within /lib/firmware).


options nouveau config="NvBIOS=quadro_fx4500.fw"

I have used this workaround on vanilla 4.1.2 kernel, it seemed to work for me on my pmac g5 quad with quadro fx4500 gpu.


As mentioned, not a fix, but a workaround...

Regards,
Peter
[/QUOTE]

[QUOTE=Linux User]
Thanks, Peter!

This actually worked... Until this issue is fixed, I will use the PC
BIOS firmware for my flashed GeForce 6200.

Again thanks for the workaround!
Cheers,
Andreas  aka  Linux User #330250
[/QUOTE]

By the way, ubuntu MATE 15.10 PowerPC works very well with 3D acceleration and sound in a chroot in fullscreen on Lubuntu 12.04.5 PowerPC. This is a fantastic possibility for users who have an older Ubuntu installed and who want to use new programs such as Firefox 41 or LibreOffice 5. It's also a possibility to test ubuntu MATE 15.10 PowerPC. ubuntu MATE 15.10 PowerPC in a chroot uses the Xorg and other hardware interfaces from the old Ubuntu system. It's not an emulated system. It's the best option for PowerPC computers where the installation of ubuntu MATE 15.10 doesn't work.

[[IMG]https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/-CtVV6Jqwudo/Vg0cI29SmQI/AAAAAAAABZk/1scx6IdvGzM/w426-h320/ubuntu_MATE_15.10_PowerPC_chroot_fullscreen.png[/IMG]]("https://plus.google.com/115515624056477014971/posts/8H1UtDv5FEM")

Edit: PLEASE test ubuntu MATE 15.10 PowerPC in a chroot.

@xeno74:

Thanks for providing that link with the detailed instructions, looks like fun.  Since you mentioned "12.04" I will once again add that 12.04 is still a very nice system for PPC and/or lower spec machines.  I have been using/testing a base xubuntu 12 install but with ToriOS/jwm DE and that combo allows my PM 3,1 with 450 MHz to do stuff online that my iBook/933 MHz unit cannot do . . . like scroll through a resource rich Facebook page.  

I'm still getting kernel updates for it, and the Tori devs are kicking up a storm with updates coming . . . frequently.  I'm waiting impatiently for their 14.04 edition to test out on the iBook . . . .  I do like MATE and have LM MATE . . . recent edition, but I think it wants more than 450 MHz to be "happy" . . . so far ToriOS is a very nice option for "older" machines . . . only thing yet to go is getting "suspend" and then it would be my main squeeze . . . .  If you are having problems with recent systems, try it . . . it is amusing to be "retro" in open source . . . . ;)

e.e.p.

### Post by ernsteiswuerfel on 2015-12-05
A couple of days ago I installed Ubuntu MATE 16.04 on my new Power Mac G5 7,3, 8 GiB RAM, Radeon 9650 mac edition, 500 GB SATA harddisc. The system is running fine so far but it feels 'sluggish' somehow. Which means keypresses and mouse gestures get swallowed randomly. And I still have to get the sound working. But apart from that no problems so far. Oh, and the "no 3d accelleration on 24bit screens with R300 hardware" is still here, so I am running xorg on a 16bit screen.

### Post by xeno74 on 2016-01-14
Hi All,

There is the latest kernel 4.4 available for the Power Mac G5. Very impressive!

Cheers,

Christian

On 14 January 2016 at 09:42 AM, Peter Saisanas wrote:
> Hi Logan,
> The kernel version is quite old (3.16.7). Perhaps you can try something newer. Nouveau continually has improvements practically with each newer kernel version.
>
> Perhaps something to consider, try the easy way out and use a pre-compiled kernel deb package that i have available. I have kernels as new as 4.4.0 available suitable for Powermac G5's.
> At least these could perhaps be a better baseline as these kernels are known to be working for many Powermac G5's (AGP & PCIe GPU's along with a few generations of nVidia GPU's (some even older than yours). Makes it easier to have a side by side comparison.
> Your call, link is below if interested.
>
> [https://drive.google.com/folderview?id=0B8pqd5Ots1vfT2puX09CYjEwcFk&usp=drive_web](https://drive.google.com/folderview?id=0B8pqd5Ots1vfT2puX09CYjEwcFk&usp=drive_web)
>
> Many have used them successfully in the past and have got their G5 Powermacs running with nouveau.
>
> I'm not so sure that MSI interrupts are ever enabled on AGP GPU's in the first place (PCIe based GPU's are a different story).
> It would be interesting to see your cat /proc/interrupts log as well.
>
> Regarding your EDID issue, can you try the other DVI connector of your video card or cable or alternatively try another display out if the issue still persists.
>
> Most Apple OEM ATI Radeon GPU's have their own issues as well. But that's another story.
>
> Regards,
> Peter
